  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_ef67b882-d42e-466a-a30e-2b152aea3011'
      });

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer310333087747820681">Kacey Cleary’s whole life imploded four years ago in a drunk-driving accident. Now she’s working hard to bury the pieces left behind—all but one. Her little sister, Livie. Kacey can swallow the constant disapproval from her born-again aunt Darla over her self-destructive lifestyle; she can stop herself from going kick-boxer crazy on Uncle Raymond when he loses the girls’ c</span>
  <span id="freeText310333087747820681" style="display:none">Kacey Cleary’s whole life imploded four years ago in a drunk-driving accident. Now she’s working hard to bury the pieces left behind—all but one. Her little sister, Livie. Kacey can swallow the constant disapproval from her born-again aunt Darla over her self-destructive lifestyle; she can stop herself from going kick-boxer crazy on Uncle Raymond when he loses the girls’ college funds at a blackjack table. She just needs to keep it together until Livie is no longer a minor, and then they can get the hell out of Grand Rapids, Michigan.<br /><br />But when Uncle Raymond slides into bed next to Livie one night, Kacey decides it’s time to run. Armed with two bus tickets and dreams of living near the coast, Kacey and Livie start their new lives in a Miami apartment complex, complete with a grumpy landlord, a pervert upstairs, and a neighbor with a stage name perfectly matched to her chosen “profession.” But Kacey’s not worried. She can handle all of them. What she can’t handle is Trent Emerson in apartment 1D.<br /><br />Kacey doesn’t want to feel. She doesn’t. It’s safer that way. For everyone. But sexy Trent finds a way into her numb heart, reigniting her ability to love again. She starts to believe that maybe she can leave the past where it belongs and start over. Maybe she’s not beyond repair.<br /><br />But Kacey isn’t the only one who’s broken. Seemingly perfect Trent has an unforgiveable past of his own; one that, when discovered, will shatter Kacey’s newly constructed life and send her back into suffocating darkness.</span>
  <a data-text-id="310333087747820681" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9703065360318253056">I have two copies of this book on my bookshelf. I only read one of them and I really, really loved it. But I felt bad that I was neglecting the other copy, so I decided to read it too, but I started with the last word and read the whole book backwards. I wouldn't recommend doing that, it doesn't really make much sense. And it takes longer to read the book back to front than it does front to back, because our brains aren't used to working in reverse. <br/>If you read this book, which I think you shoul</span>
  <span id="freeText9703065360318253056" style="display:none">I have two copies of this book on my bookshelf. I only read one of them and I really, really loved it. But I felt bad that I was neglecting the other copy, so I decided to read it too, but I started with the last word and read the whole book backwards. I wouldn't recommend doing that, it doesn't really make much sense. And it takes longer to read the book back to front than it does front to back, because our brains aren't used to working in reverse. <br />If you read this book, which I think you should, I would highly recommend reading it front to back. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15249259909269188411"><b>
  <i>"Listen......,are you breathing just a little and calling it a life?"</i>

She was a girl with auburn hair and light blue eyes - the princess of our story.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774394.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>She lived in happy times, in a happy palace of warmth, emotio</b></span>
  <span id="freeText15249259909269188411" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"Listen......,are you breathing just a little and calling it a life?"</i>
</b><br><br>How long has it been since you've read a fairytale? Let me tell you about the one I came across recently.......<b>a fairytale about redemption and forgiveness, about love and life, a fairytale about healing, about second chances.....</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774392._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774393.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> in a land not that far away lived a girl called <b>Kacey</b>. She was a girl with auburn hair and light blue eyes - the princess of our story.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774394.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>She lived in happy times, in a happy palace of warmth, emotions, and sunshine......</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774395._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But one day on her way to home with her family, best friend and boyfriend, bantering with her Dad something happened, something truly terrible, horrifying....and she had <b><i>no idea of the fate awaiting them</i>......BANG!!</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>A soft hiss ... my heart thumping in my ears. I hear nothing else. <br><br>....Mom? ...Dad? ...<br><br>Dim lights … voices …<br><br>I see them. I hear them. They’re all around, closing in. I open my mouth to scream, but I can’t find the energy. The voices get louder, the lights brighter. <b>A reedy gasp sets my hairs on end. Like a person struggling for their dying breath.</b> <br><br>I hear a loud snap, snap, snap, like someone pulling stage light levers; light suddenly pours in from all angles, illuminating the car with blinding power.<br><br>The smashed windshield.<br><br>The twisted metal.<br><br>Dark smears.<br><br>Liquid pools.<br><br>Blood. Everywhere.<br><br><b>It all suddenly disappears and I’m falling backward, crashing into cold water, sinking further into the darkness, picking up speed as the weight of an ocean swallows me whole. I open my mouth to search for air. A lungs worth of cold water greets me in a rush, filling me inside. The pressure in my chest is unbearable. It’s ready to explode. I can’t breathe....I can’t breathe......</b></i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774396.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>AND HER LIFE IS SHATTERED INTO 9 MILLION PIECES.........</i>
</b><br><br><i>
  <b>Every day is so wonderful<br>And suddenly it's hard to breathe<br>Now and then I get insecure<br>From all the pain, feel so ashamed<br><br>To all your friends you're delirious<br>So consumed in all your doom<br>Tryin' hard to fill the emptiness, the piece is gone<br>Left the puzzle undone, ain't that the way it is?</b>
</i><br><br>One, only <b>one ray of sunshine is left in her life</b>....her younger sister <b>Livie</b>.....her reason for living....<br><br>Both the sisters are as different from each other as day is from night......<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Where I’m a looming thundercloud, she’s the sunshine breaking through.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>
  <u>Livie</u>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379755073i/159671._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And for her she'd do anything......<br><br><b><u>THE FIRST MILLION PIECES</u> --<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774397.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>I've become so numb I can't feel you there. Behind my smile is a hurting heart. Behind my laugh, I'm falling apart. Look closely at me and you will see, <u>the girl I am isn't me.</u></i></b><br><br><i>If people can't deal with their problems, they numb themselves a little bit.</i> And Kacey is no different.....she makes herself numb, erects wall around her heart, creates barrier and doesn't let anyone in.....<b>the Before Kacey is lost....in the After Kacey....<i><b> <br><blockquote>I’m not Kacey Cleary anymore. I’m an empty shell who cracks inappropriate jokes and feels nothing. I’m a Kacey imposter.</blockquote></b></i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774398.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Until</b>....she meets the <b><i>Prince Charming of our story</i>, Trent</b>.....Trent with his blue blue eyes and charming dimples.....the one who with just one look crushes the walls, dismantles the barriers and lets himself in.....<br><br><b>When she sees him for the first time......</b><br><br><blockquote>
<b><i>The air leaves my lungs in a swoosh, and I’m left staring at a set of deep dimples and the bluest eyes I’ve ever seen—cobalt rings with light blue on the inside.</i></b> I squint. Do they have turquoise flecks inside them? Yes! My God! <i>The blue floors, the rusty old machines, the walls, everything around me vanishes under the weight of his gaze as it strips me of my protective bitch coat, yanking it clean off my body, <b>leaving me bare and vulnerable in seconds.</b></i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379779324i/390860._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And that is not all.....<br><br><b>Nora a.k.a. Storm</b>, her drop-dead gorgeous neighbour and her five year old daughter, <b>Mia</b>, sneak in too..........<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Mia steps out from behind her mother’s legs and wanders into our apartment, dragging a faded yellow fleece blanket behind her. At first she simply takes in our place, likely investigating for hints about her new ‘friends.’ When her eyes finally rest on Livie, they don’t shift again.<br>Livie drops to her knees to meet Mia face to face, a giant grin stretching her lips. “I’m Livie.” <b>Mia holds up her blanket, her face serious. “This is Mr. Magoo. He’s my friend.”</b></i>
</blockquote> <br><br><b>
  <u>Mia</u>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774399.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><u>THE SECOND MILLION PIECES</u>--</b><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><b>It's not denial, I'm just very selective about the reality I accept.</b><br><br>She fights, struggles to keep all of them out....tries to deny she cares........<br><br><b><u>THE THIRD MILLION PIECES</u>--</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774401._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Whatever you fight, you strengthen, and what you <u>resist</u> persists.</b><br> <br><blockquote>
  <i><b>Every fiber of my body is craving it.<br>Craving Trent.<br>I feel like I’ve come up for my first gasp of air after being under water for years.</b><br>....I’m too busy fighting this internal battle inside that tells me I must resist this charm. It’s all an act. He’s no good for me.<br><br>I fight to stay numb. That’s how I get through each day and it’s worked well for me. Until now. Now Trent has edged into my life and I can’t focus....Somehow he’s managed to slide a finger in under my titanium coat and touch me in a way that no one else has ever touched me.</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b><u>THE FOURTH MILLION PIECES</u>--</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774402._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774403.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She could never hold hands......it made her nauseous and panicky, it's her phobia, another nightmare to deal with.....the only one whose hands she could bear in hers was her sunshine, Livie,.....but someone else showed her that <b>she could grab onto his hands and he would never let go....</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I cautiously reach out, my stomach muscles coiled into a tight ball, suddenly panicked that whatever I felt earlier might be temporary, that I’ve lost it again. When my fingertips graze his and warmth spreads through me, that dread evaporates.<br><br><u>His warmth. His life.</u><br><br>Closing my eyes, I slide my hand further in, slipping my fingers between his and curling them around. My lips part in a small gasp when his grip tightens over mine. He doesn’t move closer though. He doesn’t try anything or say anything. We stand like that, in the doorway, our hands entwined, for what feels like forever.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The spaces between my fingers are right where yours fit perfectly....so hold on tight and......<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/492544.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399925ra/774404.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i><b>“I want to make you smile. For real. Always.</b> We’re going to go for dinners, and see movies, and walk on the beach. We’ll go hang-gliding, or bungee jumping, or whatever you want to do. Whatever makes you smile and laugh more.” His fingers toy with my bottom lip. <b>“Let me make you smile.”</b></i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>And so she falls......<br><br><i>Remember those walls I built<br>Well, baby they're tumbling down<br>And they didn't even put up a fight<br>They didn't even make up a sound<br><br>It's like I've been awakened<br>Every rule I had you breakin'<br><br>Everywhere I'm looking now<br>I'm surrounded by your embrace<br>Baby I can see your halo<br>You know you're my saving grace<br><br>You're everything I need and more<br>It's written all over your face<br>Baby I can feel your halo<br>Pray it won't fade away....<br> <br><u>THE FIFTH MILLION PIECES</u>--</i></b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774405._SX540_.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>I didn't hear you leave<br>I wonder, how am I still here?<br>And I don't wanna move a thing<br>It might change my memory<br><br>Oh, I am what I am<br>I'll do what I want, but I can't hide<br>And I won't go, I won't sleep, I can't breathe<br>Until you're resting here with me<br><br>And I won't leave and I can't hide, I cannot be<br>Until you're resting here with me.</b>
</i><br><br>The princess has fallen in love with the prince, they're happy together, he makes her laugh and smile but the fairytale's not over.....<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Nothing but ten tiny breaths holds the rest of me together.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The Prince has snuck in, stolen her heart, resuscitated her back to life.....for her......<i>
  <b>He’s like ripe watermelon after a lifetime of thirst. He’s like air after years under water. He’s like life.</b>
</i> But then........<br><br><b><u>THE SIXTH MILLION PIECES</u>--</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774406.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>I hold my breath, til it's more than I can take. And I close my eyes, and dream that I'm awake.</b>
</i><br><br>A shocker.....the prince has his own closet of skeletons and when the skeletons come tumbling out...everything is flooded, gone under, and the <b>princess is drowning, drowning and drowning.....</b><br><br><b><u>THE SEVENTH MILLION PIECES</u>--</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774407._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“Keep breathing. Just keep doing it. It's easy. In and out.”</i> <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I’m falling.<br>Falling backward into the deep, dark water.<br>It’s pouring over me, into me, through my mouth, up my nose, filling my lungs, seizing my will to breathe, to live.<br>I accept it. I welcome it.<br>In the distance, I hear voices. I hear people calling my name, but I can’t find them. They’re safe, above water.<br>In another world. The world of the living.<br>There’s no place for me there.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b><u>THE EIGHT MILLION PIECES</u>--</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774408.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Learn how to exhale, the inhale will take care of itself.</i>
</b><br><br><i>One … Two … Three … Four… Five… Six … Seven… Eight… Nine … Ten</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774409._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>She learns to swim, to breathe again, to live again.......<br><br><blockquote><i>I’m above water.<br>And this time I’m staying where I belong.</i></blockquote></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774410._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><u>THE NINTH MILLION PIECES</u>--</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774411.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Breathe. Let go. And remind yourself that this very moment is the only one you know you have for sure.</b><br><br>She has let go of the past........and now she seizes life....she seizes love.....<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Oh, Kace.” Trent’s lips curve and he flashes me the deepest set of dimples I’ve ever seen, buckling my knees. “Nothing’s ever been more right.”<br>That’s all I need to hear. I barrel into his arms, my mouth connecting with his.<br>Seizing him. Feeling him. Loving him.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><i>
  <b>The only thing that our hearts are made of<br>Are the acts of forgiveness and love<br>The only thing real when push comes to shove<br>Are the acts of forgiveness and love<br><br>'Cause in the end no one loses or wins<br>The story begins again and again<br>With forgiveness and love.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774413.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><u>THE TENTH WHOLE PIECE</u>: SHATTERED NO MORE; TOGETHER AGAIN--THE...</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774414.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And like any good fairytale this story ends with a happy ever after....the darkness has been conquered, the devils have been vanquished and love has triumphed once again....<br><br><i><b>"A lifetime is not what is between <br>the moments of birth and death. <br>A lifetime is one moment <br>Between my two little breaths.<br>The present, the here, the now,<br>That's all the life I get.<br>I live each moment in full,<br>In kindness, in peace, without regret."</b><br><br>And with my each breath I'll give you a happy ever after........</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774415.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774416.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The princess had never understood her mother's these words before, but now she did.....now she did.....<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Just breathe. Ten tiny breaths....<br>Seize them. <br>Feel them. <br>Love them.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774417._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399925i/774418.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>

<div id="review_1447285609" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1447285609" />
    <a title="Cristina Monica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica"><img alt="Cristina Monica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589617514p2/14596170.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1447285609?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cristina Monica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cristina Monica" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica">Cristina Monica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=death">death</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1447285609" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer91610048872762234"><br/><b>This has been a long month.</b> In truth, I will admit to having finished two novels… including this one. This has never happened before, and I hope it will never happen again. I was about to finish a third book, but <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6424171.Jurassic_Park' title='Jurassic Park by Michael Crichton' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jurassic Park</a>’s last hundred pages just don’t make me feel as excited as the previous ones.<br/><br/>Anyway, enough blabbering. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15990969.Ten_Tiny_Breaths__Ten_Tiny_Breaths___1_' title='Ten Tiny Breaths (Ten Tiny Breaths, #1) by K.A. Tucker' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ten Tiny Breaths</a> has been on my ‘‘New Adult to Read before I Die’’ list for a year before I saw it on sale on Bookoutlet.ca and thought, ‘‘meh, why not?’’ It was worth t</span>
  <span id="freeText91610048872762234" style="display:none"><br /><b>This has been a long month.</b> In truth, I will admit to having finished two novels… including this one. This has never happened before, and I hope it will never happen again. I was about to finish a third book, but <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6424171.Jurassic_Park" title="Jurassic Park by Michael Crichton" rel="nofollow noopener">Jurassic Park</a>’s last hundred pages just don’t make me feel as excited as the previous ones.<br /><br />Anyway, enough blabbering. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15990969.Ten_Tiny_Breaths__Ten_Tiny_Breaths___1_" title="Ten Tiny Breaths (Ten Tiny Breaths, #1) by K.A. Tucker" rel="nofollow noopener">Ten Tiny Breaths</a> has been on my ‘‘New Adult to Read before I Die’’ list for a year before I saw it on sale on Bookoutlet.ca and thought, ‘‘meh, why not?’’ It was worth the couple of bucks I paid for it, but it really made me realize that I should attempt fixing this bad habit I have to never read the synopsises of books! I think I’m about to read a love/hate romance story when what I get is a mystery book. I think I’m about to lose myself in a psychological thriller when what I get is a cheesy college romance story.<br /><br />Here I go again. All this to say that I had not clue this book would deal with death, lost, forgiveness and contain (clearly) a lot of psychological elements. I mean, I definitely predicted something relatively intense, but the overdone car accident leads to parents’ death, leads to emotional breakdown, leads to moving away, leads to meeting a hot guy that will save the day just didn’t take me by surprise. <br /><br />I appreciated all the background we got on Kacey, because it really helps us understand her motives better and opens our comprehensive eyes to a lot of the things she does (or did) that we normally wouldn’t approve of. Kacey is a character that is not easily defined, especially not by the place where she lives or works but it’s the <i>why</i> she lives in a crappy place and works in a strip club that are worth analysing. <br /><br />Kacey is physically strong, that can easily be said, but she’s also very stubborn and emotionally fragile. She may deny that if someone ever dares say that to her face but, believe me, she’s got this wall she built to keep everyone out, because she’s afraid that, if it crumbles, she will too. I liked her. I didn’t connect to her, because broken heroes and heroines are very hit or miss for me, but I dare say I wouldn’t mind reading another book with her in it.<br /><br />As for *trumpets* Trent, the hot and mysterious guy with gorgeous blue eyes from the laundry room, I’m going to say that I’m not displeased. Of course, I predicted the plot twist, so that’s always a down, but I didn’t mind him… Thing is, he’s pretty much like every other New Adult broken hero I’ve encountered before, except for the fact that he carries a little less of a heavy pack of anger, self-pity and self-destruction with him. Thank god.<br /><br />Livie, Storm and Mia were my sunshine in this book. I love how present they are and how their presence in the story has an actual purpose… and the fact that they get their own moment to share their story in the companion novels. I guess this is why the author doesn’t reveal <i>too</i> much about their background, although she does satisfy the reader’s curiosity. <br /><br />In sum, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15990969.Ten_Tiny_Breaths__Ten_Tiny_Breaths___1_" title="Ten Tiny Breaths (Ten Tiny Breaths, #1) by K.A. Tucker" rel="nofollow noopener">Ten Tiny Breaths</a>, while enjoyable, is not that different from the majority of New Adult books there already are out there, but, hell, it’s a structure that works and sells and that I personally keep reading because it’s hopeful. If you want unique, though, I’d recommend a New Adult Fantasy story because contemporary ones do, in my opinion, follow the same patterns over and over again. Here’s a recommendation: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22735431.The_Collectors__Society__The_Collectors__Society___1_" title="The Collectors’ Society (The Collectors’ Society, #1) by Heather Lyons" rel="nofollow noopener">The Collectors’ Society</a>!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="91610048872762234" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_467720117" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/467720117?book_show_action=true">Dec 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer467720117" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9805782809389788526"><b>Audio re-read 11/13/15. This book! Still love it just as much as the first time <3 </b><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Just breathe. Ten tiny breaths... Seize them. Feel them. Love them.</i>
</b><br/><br/>This story is absolutely beautiful. <br/><br/><i>“Our past isn’t who we are. I’m me and you’re you and that’s who we need to be.”</i><br/><br/>This is Kacey’s story<br/><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/evan%20rachel%20wood/Aguilar1998/Evan%20Rachel%20Wood/01.jpg?o=6' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399393i/772827.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>Twenty year old Kacey and her little sister Livie move to Miami, far away from their aunt and uncle in Michigan. A car accident several years ago took Kacey’s parents, best friend, and boyfriend from her a</span>
  <span id="freeText9805782809389788526" style="display:none"><b>Audio re-read 11/13/15. This book! Still love it just as much as the first time &lt;3 </b><br><br><br><b>
  <i>Just breathe. Ten tiny breaths... Seize them. Feel them. Love them.</i>
</b><br><br>This story is absolutely beautiful. <br><br><i>“Our past isn’t who we are. I’m me and you’re you and that’s who we need to be.”</i><br><br>This is Kacey’s story<br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/evan%20rachel%20wood/Aguilar1998/Evan%20Rachel%20Wood/01.jpg?o=6" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399393i/772827.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Twenty year old Kacey and her little sister Livie move to Miami, far away from their aunt and uncle in Michigan. A car accident several years ago took Kacey’s parents, best friend, and boyfriend from her and left her broken, damaged, and jaded. Kacey is a survivor. She a tough girl. All she has left is her sister. Kacey can’t cope with the loss. She tries to cope at times with drugs and sex- that doesn’t work. Now she is just getting by the best she can, going to the gym and taking care of her little sister. <br>Then theres Trent... <br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/dean%20geyer/emmataylor06/Dean%20Geyer/danielsig.jpg?o=124" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399393i/772828.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Trent is Kacey and Livie’s neighbor. Kacey starts to feel things for Trent that she hasn’t felt for years. <i>Craving Trent. I feel like I’ve come up for my first gasp of air after being under water for years.</i> Things she has never felt before. Trent is the sweetest. He is patient with Kacey and their relationship. <br><b>
  <i>“Let me make you smile.”</i>
</b><br> Loved Trent<br> Kacey also meets another neighbor, Storm and her daughter Mia. Storm was wonderful! She got Kacey a job, and tried to get to know her a befriend her. <br><i>“It’s like you’re fighting against being yourself. Every time a little bit of the real you escapes, you shut it down. Cover it up.”</i><br>Kacey is trying to do better. For herself, for her sister, and for her friends. She has people she cares about again. People she is afraid of losing. And that is terrifying for her. Her and Trent’s relationship grows. Even with a misunderstanding of him disappearing and then coming back, they are able to make it and she is finally happy. ‘Before Kacey’ as Livie would say. <br><i>He makes me happy. Happier than I’ve been in a long time. In many ways, happier than I’ve ever been. He makes me laugh. He makes me giggle. He makes me feel again. And each night, he takes my nightmares away.</i><br>Then, something happens. Things from the past resurface and no ones life will be the same. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[You just have to read it, I didn't see it coming at all- no hints! I was really shocked though! Just read it!!!!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>This is a story that will stay with you long after you read it. My heart broke for Kacey and Trent. The characters were all wonderful. This is a story of how one choice can change lives. And a story of forgiveness. <br><b>
  <i>“Because forgiveness has the power to heal.”</i>
</b><br><br>A beautiful book, loved the ending. I will defiantly be recommending this one! Bump it up on your tbr lists! <br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/holding%20hands/amiibby_/hands.jpg?o=330" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399393i/772829.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“Give me your heart, Kacey. I’ll take everything that comes with it.”<br>“I’ll make you whole again, Kacey. I promise you I will.”</i>
</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_475145257" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/475145257" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/475145257?book_show_action=true">Dec 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer475145257" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14282180936257922395">4.5 stars<br/><br/><i> <b> “Just breathe,” my mom would say.<br/>“Ten tiny breaths …<br/>Seize them.<br/>Feel them.<br/>Love them.” </b></i> <br/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400503i/776208.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i> My Trent casting^^ </i><br/><br/><b> This is a story about a girl who was drowning in the pain of her shattered life and the boy with a dark past of his own who pulled her out and helped her to breath, to live, and to love again. </b><br/><br/><i> <b> "Give me your heart, Kasey. I'll take everything that comes with it." </b></i> <br/><br/>This book doesn’t ease you in to the story, it just plunges you right in and submerges you in its beautiful and spir</span>
  <span id="freeText14282180936257922395" style="display:none">4.5 stars<br><br><i> <b> “Just breathe,” my mom would say.<br>“Ten tiny breaths …<br>Seize them.<br>Feel them.<br>Love them.” </b></i> <br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400503i/776208.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> My Trent casting^^ </i><br><br><b> This is a story about a girl who was drowning in the pain of her shattered life and the boy with a dark past of his own who pulled her out and helped her to breath, to live, and to love again. </b><br><br><i> <b> "Give me your heart, Kasey. I'll take everything that comes with it." </b></i> <br><br>This book doesn’t ease you in to the story, it just plunges you right in and submerges you in its beautiful and spiraling journey of pain, horrific loss and heart ache, and then it pulls out back up, until you feel the forgiveness and healing the characters have reached.<br><br><i> Ten Tiny Breaths </i> follows Kasey’s journey as she goes through the stages of her life, healing from trauma, finding forgiveness for unimaginable hurt, falling in love when she thought it was beyond her, and rediscovering the beauty of life.<br><br>I absolutely adored the writing style. You truly FEEL the story. You just sink right into every word you read. They are projected onto you in such a way that you have no choice but to internalize them. Feel them. Its one of those books that just has that ‘spark’, you know what I mean? That little bit of extra. This book had it. And despite the seriousness, it also had wonderful laugh out loud moment breaking up the heavy and allowing out to see another side of the characters.<br><br>After the death of her parents, best friend and boyfriend in a horrific drunk driving accident of which she was the sole survivor, and an abusive and horrible stay with their aunt and uncle, Kacey takes her sister and heads out on a bus, determined to find them a better life.<br><br>But unlike her sister, Livie, Kasey has never been a ‘good girl’. At least, not since the accident. The pain, anger and hatred at the unfairness and trauma of the event has filled her to the point where she feels numb.<br><br>So they set up in a small apartment complext in Miami and begin to piece together a new life.<br><br>Then in walks Trent. Her gorgeous god of a neighbour in 1B. He’s charming, sexy as all hell, oh, and is also 6’3″ with tattoos, an 8-pack, dimples, and a Harley… yeah… excuse me a minute while I fan myself here… But back to Trent.<br><br><i> “He skates between nice guy and bad boy so fluidly, I never seem to catch the transition.” </i><br><br>He’s the first guy in forever to make her swoon but Kasey won’t let him in at first. Her hurts run too deep and the protective walls she has built around herself are built too high. But slowly, his charm works through her defenses and she can’t help but fall for him.<br><br><i> “I swear he’s going to kiss me.<br>I swear I’m going to let him.” </i><br><br><i> <b> “I’m not ready for this. I haven’t prepared. … One… Two… Three… Four… By the time I reach ten, I’m freaking out.” </b></i> <br><br>I loved Kasey’s character and her voice. She was both damaged but strong. Her body had been broken by the accident and she had build herself back up and healed, but emotionally, she was still shattered. Angry, vulnerable, at times violent. I loved that she wasn’t held back by anyone’s judgement of her. She simply was who she was. No BS, no games.<br><br><i> <b> “I have dozens of steel pins and rods through my body, holding me together. Physically. Nothing but ten tiny breaths holds the rest of me together.” </b></i> <br><br>But she had also taken every little piece of the real her – the ‘Before Kasey’ and bottled it up. And every time a little piece of it would slip out, she’d slam a wall down ensuring it stayed locked up. Protecting herself. It was almost as if a part of her died four years before in the accident and slowly, with the help of her friends and the patience and love of this one guy, she slowly comes back to life again.<br><br>I loved that the way the writing style got you right into Kasey’s head. You became totally in sync with her thoughts and emotions. I felt like I was absolutely 100% experiencing the story right through her eyes. No disconnect ever.<br><br>I loved how the author took something as simple as the first time they held hands and was able to give it in intensity of a first kiss. Totally beautiful!<br><br><i> “I don’t know what’s happening, what I’m doing, what has taken over all rational thought, but I know I don’t want it to stop. Every fiber of my being is craving it.<br>Craving Trent.“ </i><br><br>This book really drove home how no matter what someone shows you on the outside, you never know what personal hell they are going through inside.<br><br>And then OH MY HOLY HELL! At about 40%, I put two and two together and figured out a major part of the plot twist and loved it! It gave me shivers! If I was to be picky, I’d say that I wish it had been a tad less obvious, but still, it didn’t stop me from enjoying it.<br><br>I really fell strongly for Trent. He was hiding a dark secret from his past but he was just so patient and perfect and so totally swoony! You could really feel how strongly he cared for her.<br><br><i> <b> “His dimples are in full force now. “I want to make you smile. For real. Always. We’re going to go for dinners, and see movies, and walk on the beach. We’ll go hang gliding, or bungee jumping, or whatever you want to do. Whatever makes you smile and laugh more.” His fingers toy with my bottom lip. “Let me make you smile.”<br><br>“I’d fix it all for you if I could. You know that, right?” He whispers. I wonder if he’s talking about my scars or the last four years of my life.<br>“Yes,” is all I say. Yes to all of it.“ </b></i> <br><br>I will mention that I was a just a little bit thrown by how non-graphic the bedroom scenes were. I know this is the NA genre and its not Adult, and it wasn't that the scenes were fade-to-black, but almost more that the acts were glossed over in places. You saw the immediate before and the immediate after but the actual acts were very hazy. It didn't detract from the emotional connection, but I do wish they had been just a little more present even still within the lines of NA.<br><br>The book never made me cry but I did get choked up a few times. Especially during a big tell-all scene at the end. SNIFF!<br><br>The last part of the book takes a bit of a turn from the pacing and feeling of the first part. There’s a bit of a twist to the twist, so to speak, that really makes you rethink the whole story from the beginning. I’m still trying to figure out how I feel about it. It made it… hmm… very… less perfect? hmmm, um, I don’t know really what to say but it yeah, it was unexpected to me. Really makes you think twice about the story. But I can’t say anything without spoiling it so you’ll just have to read it and see for yourself.<br><br>Don’t let that scare you off though – there is a swoony HEA with an epilogue and all so don’t worry about that!<br><br>Book #2 will be Livie’s story and I can’t wait for he story. She was such a lovable character and I’m looking forward to reading a whole book about her. I love KA Tucker’s writing style and any of her future books will be on my automatic to-buy list :)<br><br>And seriously, I think this is one of THE. BEST. COVERS. I have EVER seen!!<br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1346918160l/15990969.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14282180936257922395" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer11435455229650751069"><br/><i>How do you cope after watching your entire world crumble around you?What do you do when everything goes wrong?What do you do when pain shatters your soul?</i><br/><br/>B.R.E.A.T.H.E<br/><br/><br/><b>....................BREATHS........................<br/><br/><br/>................TINY BREATHS.......................<br/><br/><br/>.............TEN TINY BREATHS.....................<br/><br/><br/>ONE.TWO.THREE.FOUR.FIVE.SIX.SEVEN.EIGHT.NINE.TEN<br/><br/><br/>Seize them......Feel them......Love them.<br/><br/><br/>Just Breathe..........</b><br/><br/>-----------------------------------------------------------<br/><br/><i>...Mom?...D</i></span>
  <span id="freeText11435455229650751069" style="display:none"><br /><i>How do you cope after watching your entire world crumble around you?What do you do when everything goes wrong?What do you do when pain shatters your soul?</i><br /><br />B.R.E.A.T.H.E<br /><br /><br /><b>....................BREATHS........................<br /><br /><br />................TINY BREATHS.......................<br /><br /><br />.............TEN TINY BREATHS.....................<br /><br /><br />ONE.TWO.THREE.FOUR.FIVE.SIX.SEVEN.EIGHT.NINE.TEN<br /><br /><br />Seize them......Feel them......Love them.<br /><br /><br />Just Breathe..........</b><br /><br />-----------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><i>...Mom?...Dad?<br /><br />Jenny?<br /><br />Too dark to see Billy,but I know he's there because I can feel his hand.It's big and strong and it envelops mine.But it's not moving...<br /><br />The smashed windshield.<br />The twisted metal.<br />Dark smears.<br />Liquid pools.<br />Blood.Everywhere.<br /><br />It all suddenly disappears and I'm falling backward,crashing into cold water,sinking further into the darkness,picking up speed as the weight of the ocean swallows me whole......</i><br /><br /><br />-----------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>Hello Readers!!</b><br /><br />I'm in quite a fix.What do I tell you about this story? How do I explain to you the what are these ten little breaths? Why ten? Why tiny? Why not deep?<br /><br />Well our Kacey asks the same exact questions.They don't work.But she takes them anyways.That's a little bit of her mom left with her.<br /><br /><br />The story starts with 20 year old Kacey and her 15 year old sister Livie arriving in Miami.After the accident which resulted in their parent's death along with Kacey's best friend Jenny and boyfriend Billy,their custody had been handed over to their aunt and uncle.But when one drunken night their uncle makes a pass at Livie,Kacey packs up their suitcases and they come to Miami to start a new life.<br /><br />There in their new apartment they meet their neighbours Storm and her five year old daughter Mia.<br /><br />Also Kacey meets with their sexy,beautiful and smoldering hot neighbour Trent.<br /><br /><br />No one looking at these two beautiful people will ever guess how very damaged they are.<br /><br />The Kacey before the accident is dead and buried.Now all she has is pain and anger and hatred.Which she channels out during kickboxing.Yes,she can kick some serious ass.<br /><br />But unbeknownst to her,somehow Mia,Storm,Trent manage to creep in.<br /><br />And nothing is more vulnerable than LOVE.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Isn't it exhausting?" The pad of thumb strokes my neck softly.<br />"What?"<br />"Keeping people out."</i>
</b><br /><br />But how can she keep him out when he breaks down her every defence?<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I want to make you smile.For real.Always.We're going to go for dinners,and see movies,and walk on the beach.We'll go hang-gliding,or bungee jumping,or whatever you want to do.Whatever makes you laugh and smile more.His fingers toy with my botom lip,"Let me make you smile."</i>
</b><br /><br />And so the girl who had sworn off love,falls crazily in love.<br /><br />The girl who hated to be vulnerable,becomes vulnerable.<br /><br />And the girl who never let any one hold her hands after Billy died holding them,lets him hold them!!<br /><br />But...Trent has his own secrets.Secrets which can tear them apart....<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I hope one day you can heal from all of this,and someone can make you laugh.You have such a beautiful laugh,Kacey Cleary."</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>So Readers,join Kacey in the nine stages of her life---<br /><br /><i>Stage One--Comfortably Numb <br />Stage Two--Denial <br />Stage Three--Resistance <br />Stage Four--Acceptance <br />Stage Five--Dependence <br />Stage Six--Withdrawal <br />Stage Seven--Breakdown<br />Stage Eight--Recovery<br />Stage Nine--Forgiveness</i><br /><br />Join Kacey and experience the healing which occurs when you let the hatred go.<br /><br />The healing of soul which only forgiveness can bring.<br /><br />And come and learn with Kacey **WHY TEN LITTLE BREATHS**!!<br /><br />And watch her resurface....TO LIFE!!</b><br /><br /><i>I barrel into his arms,my mouth connecting with his.<br /><br />Seizing him.Feeling him.Loving him.</i><br /><br /><b>That's all for now.<br />Ta-Ta!!</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5385432907745294816">This book was a fucking mess. There was NOTHING about it that I enjoyed. The main character was a bitch, the entire book's premise was unrealistic and disgusting, the romance was dry, rushed, and unrealistic, there was slut shaming, etc. NOTHING in this book made sense. I am appalled someone read this and went "!!!! wow!!!!! let's publish this!!!!!" the storyline was so predictable and cheesy and the relationship was SO gross and toxic, and the entire construction of this book was a trainwreck. </span>
  <span id="freeText5385432907745294816" style="display:none">This book was a fucking mess. There was NOTHING about it that I enjoyed. The main character was a bitch, the entire book's premise was unrealistic and disgusting, the romance was dry, rushed, and unrealistic, there was slut shaming, etc. NOTHING in this book made sense. I am appalled someone read this and went "!!!! wow!!!!! let's publish this!!!!!" the storyline was so predictable and cheesy and the relationship was SO gross and toxic, and the entire construction of this book was a trainwreck.     <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_489117209" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/489117209" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/489117209?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781476740331" href="/book/show/17278200-ten-tiny-breaths">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Stacia (the 2010 club) by: </span>
      Read with Archaeologist's Anonymous group
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=new-adult-college">new-adult-college</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer489117209" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3250286630065997304"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Old MacKacey had a farm. E-I-E-I-O. <br/>And on this farm she had a Trent. E-I-E-I-O.<br/>With a wink, wink, here and a smirk, smirk, there. Here a wink, there a wink, everywhere a wink, wink.<br/>Old MacKacey had a farm. E-I-E-I-OOOOOOOOOOHHHHHHHHHHH...</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><b>2.5 stars.</b> Sleepy Stacia after a long weekend = nothing in the bag of tricks other than some random thoughts. I'll avoid non-tagged major spoilers of specific outcome-revealing details, but there will probably be dancing around general plot points o</span>
  <span id="freeText3250286630065997304" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Old MacKacey had a farm. E-I-E-I-O. <br />And on this farm she had a Trent. E-I-E-I-O.<br />With a wink, wink, here and a smirk, smirk, there. Here a wink, there a wink, everywhere a wink, wink.<br />Old MacKacey had a farm. E-I-E-I-OOOOOOOOOOHHHHHHHHHHH...</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><b>2.5 stars.</b> Sleepy Stacia after a long weekend = nothing in the bag of tricks other than some random thoughts. I'll avoid non-tagged major spoilers of specific outcome-revealing details, but there will probably be dancing around general plot points of the book and commentating on some of the events. <br /><br />I'm going to give my final verdict upfront : I liked <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i> enough to read all the way through. This was mainly because of my curiosity to see how Kacey would fare, as well as what would happen with Mia, Storm, and Livie. I did not like the character of Trent. At ALL. He would wink and smirk and wink and smirk. He never really showed anything of himself until pretty far into the book (just showing up, hanging around, and looking hot is not enough for me). Kacey observed from the get-go that it seemed like he knew something was wrong with her and yet she never questioned why he was always there, wanting to help? I get grief being a cloud but what was it about Trent which made her decide to let her guard down? I'm not sure if this was ever made clear.<br /><br />Trent was a stalker. Kacey went from shutting the entire world out to changing her tune just because of dual-colored eyes. Although, I guess if I ever saw someone with turquoise flecks in their eyes, I might cave too because that's pretty damn unusual. Is he a supernatural creature? Maybe so, because guess what ladies...he can make you climax with just a look. No, I'm not kidding. I wish I were. I actually went and flipped back and forth a few pages to try and find out what made Kacey deduce that Trent was a "godlike creature" who "couldn't be a creep because he was too beautiful and too nice." Uh, what scene did I miss there? A brief encounter in the laundry room and a couple minutes of conversation? <br /><br />So how does the relationship build, you ask? Is it through long and meaningful conversations and poignant moments? Uh, no. Trent decides to show up at the strip club where Kacey works at and stare at her. Rinse, repeat...for shift after shift. Then in one of the few brief 'alone' moments, he comes up with this question -<br /><b>"Isn't it exhausting?"<br />"What?"<br />"Keeping people out."</b><br />Maybe I'm too world-weary but if someone said that to me and I barely knew them, I'd probably laugh and say "who are you to assume that you know anything about me?" then walk away. <br /><br />Now, the stalking might have been kind of cute if Kacey worked at the local IHOP (that's a restaurant for those who don't have them where they live) and he showed up on occasion to order his morning coffee before heading off to work. But, nope. Avoiding the naked chicks so you can watch the chick at the bar serve drinks to horny men was just...bizarre? <br /><br />Oh, btw...Kacey got job at said bar with no test of her knowledge on how to make drinks, no trial run or training, and no paperwork. It was 'here's a rec from a friend' and she's in there working right away. Hey, I'm no bar expert, but I'd assume the person hiring would want to know if you can even make some basic drinks and might watch you for a sec? <br /><br />So when stalker guy finally gets close, these are the words which are supposed to make things better?<br /><b>"I'll make you whole again, Kacey. I promise you, I will," he whispers.</b><br />Back the train up here. She's aware of the fact that when you're broken inside, another person can't make you whole, right? At least, she should be aware that another person can't banish your own personal demons (even if they can help you through the process as you learn to do it yourself).<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Her thoughts one paragraph later : <b>Pushing inside me, making me whole.</b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />*Stacia lays her head down on the desk and tries out this 'ten tiny breaths' technique as shown in the book*<br /><br />I felt like the 'twist' was unnecessary and turned a touching story about one person's emotional recovery into something wrong, twisted, and useful only for the purpose of shock value. I guessed what was coming when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Trent kept harping on how he was going to fix her. Why would this person who didn't even know her be so invested in needing to fix her unless he had a connection? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> So when it happened, I sort of groaned out loud and wished that things had gone differently. Why couldn't <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Trent have just been a normal guy who helped Kacey learn to start living again? Instead, we find out that he was just as screwed up as she was and that they were going to somehow try to work together to form a functioning relationship? Realistically, the book would have been better had Trent been put back into the hospital and he and Kacey never saw each other again. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Because of my complaints, the ending bugged me. It was too easily solved. I don't mind "issues" books having a strong presence of romance but the romance needs to make sense. And this romance never quite made sense, given that these two people didn't ever really know each other.<br /><br /><b>So where are my positives?</b><br /><br /><i>The story was actually</i> readable. <i>The story was actually</i> interesting. <i>The story was actually</i> moving at times. The secondary characters <i>absolutely</i> made the book for me and I'm glad that they were there. <br /><br />This book would have been AWESOME if the Storm/Kacey friendship had been the focus because the friendship part of the story was my favorite part. It's always nice to see when females can put away initial misgivings and learn to trust one another because this can be such a rare thing in the real world. If Storm (or Livie) had helped Kacey start to put the pieces back together instead of Trent, this could have been a "wow" book for me. Never, have I ever wished so much for a romance to go away than I have with this book. I would have loved to have seen a person find reasons to keep moving and keep seeking out help, other than through the urging of a 'godlike male.' The book was a good read but it could have been a great read without the romance...or if the romantic lead had come in much later in the book, after Kacey had already started the healing process, and been there for her through the later stages of recovery.<br /><br /><b>Who might like this book?</b> I'd say that it would work for just about anyone who loves books where romance is the primary focus. As a straight-forward love story (without picking apart the details like I have), it works. Even though I do enjoy romance, I generally put the story as a whole over the aspect of romance, so <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i> only worked halfway for me. I expected more than what I got. <br /><br />Stacia's prediction : I see a future movie deal in the style of a Nicholas Sparks flick. Horrified men will be dragged along by their girlfriends to watch this on the big screen. Women will cry. Men will keep checking the time on their phones. I'm calling it now. <br /><br /><br /><i>This book provided from the publisher through Netgalley in exchange for an honest review.</i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3250286630065997304" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_471292459" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/471292459" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/471292459?book_show_action=true">Dec 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16700492-ten-tiny-breaths">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=swoonworthy-male-lead">swoonworthy-male-lead</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=tearjerkers">tearjerkers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=emotional-rollercoaster">emotional-rollercoaster</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer471292459" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5170033667035075506"><i>"A hissing sound..<br/>Bright lights...<br/>And then it all just...stops. And I'm vaguely aware that something is very wrong. "Mom? Dad?" There's no answer. <br/>It's hard to breathe..."</i><br/><br/><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399926ra/774432.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><br/><blockquote>
  <b>"Just breathe," my mom would say. "Ten tiny breaths..."</b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399926i/774433.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>~ Seize them.<br/>~ Feel them. <br/>~ Love them.</b><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/460210.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p> <i>And that is exactly what Kacey does every time she feels like the world has fallen form underneath her feet and she just can't breath any more...</i><br/><br/><b>Ten tiny breaths</b> is a remarkable story about loss, love, friendship and about </span>
  <span id="freeText5170033667035075506" style="display:none"><i>"A hissing sound..<br>Bright lights...<br>And then it all just...stops. And I'm vaguely aware that something is very wrong. "Mom? Dad?" There's no answer. <br>It's hard to breathe..."</i><br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399926ra/774432.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Just breathe," my mom would say. "Ten tiny breaths..."</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399926i/774433.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>~ Seize them.<br>~ Feel them. <br>~ Love them.</b><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/460210.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p> <i>And that is exactly what Kacey does every time she feels like the world has fallen form underneath her feet and she just can't breath any more...</i><br><br><b>Ten tiny breaths</b> is a remarkable story about loss, love, friendship and about losing everything you have in life and learning how to pick up the pieces to make it whole again... And in the end, isn't that what life is all about? Falling down, and learning to get back up again? I think we all go through the stages of recovery at least once in our lives, but everyone handles with them in their own way. In this book, the mantra that's continuously repeated to regain control over your life is to take <i>ten tiny breaths</i>... Does this mantra help at all?? Why ten? Why tiny and not deep? <i>That</i> is what you'll have to find out for yourself by reading this wonderful story...<br><br><b>Ten Tiny Breaths</b> follows the journey of a girl named <b>Kacey Cleary--</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379774896i/335762._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When we first meet Kacey, she's not the same person she used to be four years ago... Four years ago, is when a terrible car accident happened and Kacey did not only lose the four most important people in her life (her mom, her dad, her best friend and her boyfriend), she also lost a very important part of <b>herself</b>. She suffered from the accident; not only physically (her body now being covered in scars and held together by dozens of metal rods and pins); but most of all she suffered emotionally...<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Before Kacey died four years ago and all that's left is a mess. A mess who spent a year in physical rehabilitation to repair her shattered body, only to be released with a shattered soul. <br><br>I'm not Kacey Cleary anymore. I'm an empty shell who cracks inappropriate jokes and feels nothing. I'm Kacey imposter."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Emotionally all that holds her together are <i>
  <b>ten tiny breaths</b>
</i> every time she feels panic rising... <br><br>After her parents died, Kacey and her sister Livie spent four years living with their aunt and uncle but after their uncle tries to assault Livie; the two sisters decide to move out and start a new life in Miami.<br><br>And that is were Kacey meets her new next-door-neighbor <b>Trent--</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399926i/774434._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At first he's <i>
  <b>a contradiction. One second sweet, the next second brazen. A mind-blowing hot contradiction.</b>
</i><br><br>But Kacey and Trent quickly become inseparable and although Kacey has an impenetrable shield wrapped tightly around her heart, Trent manages to break through, slowly but surely... He makes her want to be <b>alive</b> again. <br><blockquote>
  <i>"Something's just different with Trent. He's like watermelon after a lifetime of thirst. He's like air after years under water. <u>He's like life..."</u></i>
</blockquote>Because of Trent, Kacey finally allows people back into her heart...<br><br>So we follow Kacey along the journey of healing... We follow her through the nine stages that will make her life whole again - <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Stage One ~ Comfortably Numb<br>Stage Two ~ Denial<br>Stage Three ~ Resistance<br>Stage Four ~ Acceptance<br>Stage Five ~ Dependence<br>Stage Six ~ Withdrawal<br>Stage Seven ~ Breakdown<br>Stage Eight ~ Recovery<br>Stage Nine ~ Forgiveness</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><i>I've learned that the process of healing isn't an easy one... In fact it's a very hard one and you'll probably struggle a lot, but with the right people by your side, anything is possible...</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I want to make you smile. For real. Always. We're going to go for dinners, and see movies, and walk on the beach. We'll go hang gliding, or bungee jumping, or whatever you want to do. Whatever makes you smile and laugh more. Let me make you smile."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399926ra/774435.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Give me your heart, Kacey. I'll take everything that comes with it."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399926ra/774436.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Inhaling, I look up into his face and see a world of calm and possibilities. For the first time in four years, the thought of a hand covering mine doesn't send me into a dizzying spiral down. And I realize that I want Trent to touch me."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399926ra/774437.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br>Reading this story made me <i><b>cry</b> over all the sadness these young people had to go through, <br>it made me <b>laugh</b> at all of Kacey's sarcastic and hilarious remarks, <br>it <b>warmed my heart</b> to see such a strong bond between Kacey and her sister Livie, <br>it made me <b>smile</b> at how in love Kacey in Trent were <br>and it made me <b>hope</b> for a better life for all these wonderful characters because they sure deserved it... <br>It was a beautiful, unforgettable story and it definitely earned itself a very special place in my heart...</i><br><br>And now I can't wait to read <u>Livie's story</u> in the upcoming sequel <b>
  <u>One Tiny Lie</u>
</b>... K.A. Tucker, you've gained yourself a new fan!!! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399926i/774438.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>5 HEARTWARMING STARS!!!</b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_478920770" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/478920770" />
    <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews"><img alt="Tough Critic Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345668583p2/5336035.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/478920770?book_show_action=true">Dec 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer478920770" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer590737156264415527">This was another read in which I was doused with reader hype before I had a chance to pick it up. When that's the case, I try not to expect much. Actually, I prefer to enter a book with little to no expectations. Expectations tend to taint my experience. However, if you look up synonyms for taint you'll find the word infect. There is no doubt that I was infected by <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i> from the very first moment. <br/><br/>What blew my mind was that this book was a fast paced easy read despite the trauma, hea</span>
  <span id="freeText590737156264415527" style="display:none">This was another read in which I was doused with reader hype before I had a chance to pick it up. When that's the case, I try not to expect much. Actually, I prefer to enter a book with little to no expectations. Expectations tend to taint my experience. However, if you look up synonyms for taint you'll find the word infect. There is no doubt that I was infected by <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i> from the very first moment. <br /><br />What blew my mind was that this book was a fast paced easy read despite the trauma, heartache, loss, and pain. It was a complete contradiction. It was the perfect contradiction. Don't get me wrong, I love when a book takes over my heart and crushes me with so much emotion I can't breathe, but sometimes...I want to breathe. I was not suffocated or drowned by the emotion or drama, but I was able to experience it and at the same time enjoy it. It was not overpowering; it was perfect.<br /><br />The tension between Kacey and Trent is palpable. My only issue was the semi-awkwardness of the beginning of their relationship. Specifically the second laundromat scene. I loved how their relationship wasn't rushed, but that's exactly what made Trent's "You are so very beautiful" comment seem a little out of place...awkward even. Other than that I loved everything about Trent and Kacey. <br /><br />The other mind blowing experience of <i>Ten Tiny Breaths</i> was the secondary characters. <i>All</i> of the secondary characters. So much love! It was like a secondary character orgy. Storm, Mia, Tanner, Caine, Brad, Nate, and Dan. I. Loved. Them. All. Caring about these characters helped make this such a fast read. It caused me to be completely invested in such a way that I never, never had any bored moments...no draggy bits. <br /><br />I admit, I knew about halfway through what the "big secret" was, but I didn't care. I still enjoyed the experience of getting there. I would have loved to see a little more out of the ending (specifically Trent and Kacey's beginning...together), but again, I think it was more about me not wanting to let these characters go. I was pulled into their world, their stories, their heartache, their love, their loss, and their healing. I didn't want to leave. <br /><br />I definitely recommend it! READ ON!</span>
  <a data-text-id="590737156264415527" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
