<div id="review_1409734103" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1409734103" />
    <a title="Ophelia&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47653844-ophelia-s-book-blog"><img alt="Ophelia&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448312511p2/47653844.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1409734103?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ophelia&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ophelia&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/47653844-ophelia-s-book-blog">Ophelia&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1409734103" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14900207666992688299">: <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444419119i/16497991._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='180' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Ten Tiny Breaths by K.A. Tucker<br/><br/> <b>
  <blockquote>"I want to make you smile. For real. Always. We’re going to go for dinners, see movies, and walk on the beach. We’ll go hang-gliding, or bungee jumping, or whatever you want to do. Whatever makes you smile and laugh more. Let me make you smile."</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>This book was recommended to me by so many readers and everyone was raving about it, it had so much hype surrounding it. When I decided to see what the fuss was about I naturally had high expectations that I tried rea</span>
  <span id="freeText14900207666992688299" style="display:none">: <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444419119i/16497991._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Ten Tiny Breaths by K.A. Tucker<br><br> <b>
  <blockquote>"I want to make you smile. For real. Always. We’re going to go for dinners, see movies, and walk on the beach. We’ll go hang-gliding, or bungee jumping, or whatever you want to do. Whatever makes you smile and laugh more. Let me make you smile."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>This book was recommended to me by so many readers and everyone was raving about it, it had so much hype surrounding it. When I decided to see what the fuss was about I naturally had high expectations that I tried really hard to squash because high expectations are never a good thing to have going into a book. <br><br>The story is about Kacey Cleary a twenty-year- old girl who was in a car accident that killed both of her parents, her boyfriend and her best friend. After the tragic event her aunt who was a bible fanatic got custody of Kacey and her little sister Livie.<br>Kacey suffered from severe PTSD (Post Traumatic Stress Disorder) and at first tried to cope by using drugs, drinking and being promiscuous after that didn’t work, she found a more effective way which was kickboxing at the gym.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444419313i/16497996._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br> One night, after her uncle came home drunk and tried to molest Livie, they packed up and left. And that’s where the book starts; they rent an apartment in Miami, where they meet Nora AKA Storm a single mother to an adorable 5 year old, Trent the hot mysterious neighbor and Tanner the landlord and they form a little family.<br><br><br>Surprisingly it was a really fast paced book; I finished it in one sitting. The angst was there but it wasn’t overwhelming or too over the top. It was just right.<br><br><br>I didn’t love the writing style very much because I felt like the author was telling me the story more than showing it to me, I didn’t feel connected to the characters at times and that bothered me.<br><br>Kacey was a very damaged character, jaded and just plain screwed up. She was too judgmental at times and that made me dislike her a little bit. She kept a protective bubble around herself not letting anyone in, and pushing away everyone who tried to get close, afraid of getting hurt. Men didn’t interest her anymore physically or otherwise until Trent. There was something about him.<br><br> <b>
  <blockquote>“The way he takes over a room, the way he looks at me, like he has already identified and can disarm every one of my defense mechanisms with no effort like he sees through them to the disaster lying beneath.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Trent was a great guy, he was patient, sweet, and he wanted so badly to “fix” Kacey. He had a dark past of his own that he to deal with and it made him so mysterious. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444419545i/16498024.jpg" width="200" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>
  <blockquote>“What’s wrong is that every morning and every night, I lie in bed wondering why you’re not beside me.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>He tried to make her deal with her past so she could move on. He pushed her to talk about the things that she buried.<br>Their relationship was intense hot and very passionate.<br><br> <b>
  <blockquote>“Isn't it exhausting?"<br>"What?"<br>"Keeping people out.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>This is a story about loss, suffering, healing and forgiveness.<br><br> <b>Rating: 3.5 Stars</b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14900207666992688299" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

Tucker. Of course since I had used up all of my lib</span>
  <span id="freeText1016325598206878998" style="display:none">Find all of my reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/">http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>^^^^This one did it for me. In case we haven’t yet met . . . . <br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472574958ra/20210213.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For real – but I do try and pick out books that I won't hate. I got denied a reader copy of this book waaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaay back in the Fall of ’13 and promptly forgot all about it. Then a few weeks ago I <s>was stalking her Facebook page</s> noticed <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1260020109?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Tarryn Fisher</a> had just read/recommended <i>He Will Be My Ruin</i> by K.A. Tucker. Of course since I had used up all of my librarian requests making sure the pornography collection was well-stocked, that book wasn’t available. However, this one was and I figured same author probably still good, right? Wrong. <br><br>Alright, so here’s the plot: Kasey and her sister Livie were orphaned when their parents were killed in a drunk-driving accident (Kasey was the only survivor in the car, Livie was home with the flu and wasn’t in the accident at all). Fast forward a few years and Kasey and Livie hightailing it to Miami after their creeper of an uncle “accidentally” climbed into bed with Livie. The two set up residence in a “Melrose Place” style apartment complex and begin to move on with their lives. And then Kasey meets the new boy next door . . . . <br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472574958ra/20210214.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And panties be dropppppppppping! <br><br>Okay, it’s NA so panties be dropping after a whole lotta angst and in fade-to-black style, but they still be dropping. Oh and there’s instalove. Of course. Chick meets dude in the laundry room, immediately runs away because she has some wicked PTSD that she’s never dealt with due to watching nearly everyone she loved die around and she’s scurrrrred of feeling the feels but then fast-forward a couple of weeks later to . . . <br><br><b>
  <i>“Somehow he’s managed to slide a finger under my titanium coat and touch me in a way that no one else ever has.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472574958ra/20210215.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Seriously. At that point they hadn’t even really had a conversation, but whatevs. Young love.<br><br>Then things get even more convoluted and magic peen goes all Coldplay and declares that “lights will guide you home – and ignite your bones – and I will tryyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyy to fix you.” (&lt;&lt;&lt; not a Coldplay fan, but that is a farking excellent song). The big dun dun dunnnnnnnn moment was glaring like a fiery G.D. beacon to me and once my thoughts were confirmed I was all . . . . <br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472574958ra/20210216.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This one just WAS. NOT. FOR. ME. At all. But that’s what I get for diving back in the NA pool headfirst even though I should know better. I’d give it 1 Star, but I’ve been trolled enough (by the granny faction of Goodreads, no less) in recent weeks and I’m not really interested in garnering the attention of Tucker’s fangirls. Also, that cover?????<br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472574958i/20210217.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>That’s worthy of a star all by itself. Look at me and my Grinch heart being all generous and shit! <br><br><i>ARC denied eleven thousand years ago by NetGalley, but I still read it anyway.</i><br><br>EPILOGUE: In a wondrous turn of events my bemoaning the first world problem which is my lack of dollars and ginormous library fail regarding the K.A. Tucker book I <b>really</b> wanted to read, I was bequeathed it by a delightful little book fairy . . . <br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_536959427" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/536959427" />
    <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga"><img alt="Beatrice Masaluñga" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603719912p2/4590441.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/536959427?book_show_action=true">Aug 08, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beatrice Masaluñga" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga">Beatrice Masaluñga</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Beatrice by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/6756655-jan-bethel">Jan Bethel</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536959427" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15791177597644172644">Four years ago, a tragic accident happened that killed her parents, friend and boyfriend traumatized <b>Kacey Cleary</b>. She's damaged and her nightmares continued to haunt her. She and her younger sister, Livie are living with their Aunt Darla - a born-again christian and Uncle Raymond - who gambled their college funds and lost it. She refused to get help on her PTSD and she almost destroy herself by doing drugs, drinking alcohol and having hook-ups as means of coping which are unacceptable to her au</span>
  <span id="freeText15791177597644172644" style="display:none">Four years ago, a tragic accident happened that killed her parents, friend and boyfriend traumatized <b>Kacey Cleary</b>. She's damaged and her nightmares continued to haunt her. She and her younger sister, Livie are living with their Aunt Darla - a born-again christian and Uncle Raymond - who gambled their college funds and lost it. She refused to get help on her PTSD and she almost destroy herself by doing drugs, drinking alcohol and having hook-ups as means of coping which are unacceptable to her aunt. One night, her drunk uncle slipped to Livie's bed that scared the heck out of her sister was a wake up call for them to leave Michigan and move to Miami where they can start a new life. <br /><br />They live on a small apartment just enough for them and their neighbors are warm and friendly, like Storm and her little daughter Mia. At first, Kacey is really aloof but tries her best to engage in conversations. Still, she puts her guard up and doesn't want to talk about her past. But there's something about her sexy,attractive neighbor, <b>Trent Emerson</b>, stirs her emotions. Being around him makes her comfortable and undeniably, they're attracted with each other. Slowly, she's falling for him and she wants to love someone again. What if she's not the only one who's broken? It seems Trent has a traumatic past and the truth might ruin Kacey again.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Ten tiny breaths...Seize them. Feel them. Love them."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />This has been on my TBR for ages. Goodness, I wish I've read this earlier. <b>The heroine has a great character development.</b> Kacey might be a tough nut to crack but she's a selfless, independent and responsible woman for taking care of her sister. Talking about the past makes her vulnerable but for the sake of the people who care and love her, she conquered by seeking help in order to forgive and heal the scars that damaged her. It's not easy but seeing her happy makes me want to cheer her. <b>I really like the plot twist.</b> I almost guess it right with some clues and all but I'm still a little shock by it.. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I'm suspicious that Trent is part of the accident but I didn't expect he is Cole. Hahah! I almost got it. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> haha! <b>I love the chemistry between Kacey and Trent</b>. They shared some steamy scenes enough to make me feel giddy as they take their relationship slow. I like how Trent is more patient than Kacey (can't blame her raging hormones. Trent is HAWT). All the conflicts were resolved and I'm satisfied on how it ends. Definitely no loopholes. <br /><br />Overall, I really enjoyed this book and it's a great start for the series. I am looking forward to read the rest of it. </span>
  <a data-text-id="15791177597644172644" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1733105727" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1733105727" />
    <a title="Beth Hudspeth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18107143-beth-hudspeth"><img alt="Beth Hudspeth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1495723320p2/18107143.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1733105727?book_show_action=true">Aug 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beth Hudspeth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beth Hudspeth" href="/user/show/18107143-beth-hudspeth">Beth Hudspeth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18107143-beth-hudspeth?shelf=2016-reads">2016-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18107143-beth-hudspeth?shelf=book-reviews">book-reviews</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1733105727" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10406885746405808162"><b>Reviewed by</b>: <a href='https://hellobeautifulbookblog.com/2016/10/26/book-review-ten-tiny-breaths-by-k-a-tucker/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Hello Beautiful Book Blog</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Passionate story with twists along the way. Must read for new adult romance fans. This author ranks with some of the best.</i>
</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>Just breathe, Kacey. Ten tiny breaths. Seize them. Feel them. Love them.</i>
</blockquote><br/>My first book by K.A. Tucker. I always like to start at the beginning with an author when I can. That way you can see how far they’ve come as an artist. Am I alone in that or does everyone like to do that?<br/><br/>This starts out as your typical romance. Girl moves to </span>
  <span id="freeText10406885746405808162" style="display:none"><b>Reviewed by</b>: <a href="https://hellobeautifulbookblog.com/2016/10/26/book-review-ten-tiny-breaths-by-k-a-tucker/" rel="nofollow noopener">Hello Beautiful Book Blog</a><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Passionate story with twists along the way. Must read for new adult romance fans. This author ranks with some of the best.</i>
</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>Just breathe, Kacey. Ten tiny breaths. Seize them. Feel them. Love them.</i>
</blockquote><br />My first book by K.A. Tucker. I always like to start at the beginning with an author when I can. That way you can see how far they’ve come as an artist. Am I alone in that or does everyone like to do that?<br /><br />This starts out as your typical romance. Girl moves to new city, meets boy and romance ensues. Except, there are some serious twists along the way. I loved that Kacey wasn’t your typical herione and didn’t follow what people thought she should be doing. She is independent almost to a fault.<br /><br />I really loved Kacey’s relationship with Storm. I love when girls look out for one another. Their bond was strong. Kacey has a hard time letting people in or caring about people in general, but Storm easily opened her up to their friendship. She was so helpful with getting Kacey a decent paying job and making sure her and Livie were taken care of.<br /><br />Trent Emerson is the perfect love interest. He is mysterious in the best way, but also thoughtful and protective. I found Trent to be a little too protective at times. I know he means well, but I kept thinking he was being a creep. I ended up really liking his character. He and Kacey are bound together and I love that. Trent and Kacey harbor a very special connection and I don’t think that should be taken lightly.<br /><br />Kacey Cleary’s story is filled with cheese and unbelievable senarios, however Tucker does a wonderful job of making you not care. Storylines with far fetched plots must be treaded on carefully. I felt Tucker made the characters real enough that you found yourself making excuses for the events surrounding the plot. I thought this was a well executed book and would very much like to read more of K.A. Tucker’s work to see how she has grown as an author.<br /><br />There were some major things that I felt were wrong with this book and some things I did not agree with whatsoever, but the writing style of K.A. Tucker outweighed much of every complaint I had. She is such a strong storyteller, as I was turning each page I couldn’t help but love this book.<br /><br />What did y’all think about this one?</span>
  <a data-text-id="10406885746405808162" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16700492-ten-tiny-breaths">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer540410187" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18358931501175820670">Wow - must say this one was very good. So many talented new authors out there now. Saw where it was going to go while reading it but still did not take away anything from the story. Loved the main characters. Poor Kacey, trying to be a tough nut. Trent, what's not to love about him and of course the extended "family" - Storm, Mia .... Think we might get Livie's story at some stage - Hopefully. It was sad, happy, funny, sad but it got there in the end. Just breathe!<br/><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410311i/804376.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></span>

<div id="review_1417671495" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1417671495" />
    <a title="Michelle " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23450274-michelle"><img alt="Michelle " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1544751386p2/23450274.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1417671495?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle " href="/user/show/23450274-michelle">Michelle </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23450274-michelle?shelf=college">college</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23450274-michelle?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1417671495" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12394509584834911929">5 Stars!<br/>Loved this book! I was up all night reading this one because I needed to finish it. <br/><br/>“Take ten tiny breaths. Seize them. Feel them. Love them.”<br/><br/>That's what Kacey's mom used to tell her to do when things got tough. Kacey doesn't understand whatever her mom was trying to tell her. Nothing will help her right now. Ten tiny breaths are defiantly not going to make things better. Kacey is fine being the mean, angry and sarcastic girl. She doesn't need or want anything in her life except her sist</span>
  <span id="freeText12394509584834911929" style="display:none">5 Stars!<br />Loved this book! I was up all night reading this one because I needed to finish it. <br /><br />“Take ten tiny breaths. Seize them. Feel them. Love them.”<br /><br />That's what Kacey's mom used to tell her to do when things got tough. Kacey doesn't understand whatever her mom was trying to tell her. Nothing will help her right now. Ten tiny breaths are defiantly not going to make things better. Kacey is fine being the mean, angry and sarcastic girl. She doesn't need or want anything in her life except her sister Livie. <br /><br />Kacey is no longer the outgoing, funny, flirty and friendly girl she was at 16. She goes through life now avoiding others touch. <br /><br />The very idea of my hands wrapped in someone else’s has plagued me, making my heart stop, my stomach drop, my vision blurry, my muscles spasm, and sweat pour down my back all at once. Until now. ~Kacey<br /><br />When Kacey runs into her new neighbor Trent she can't help but to want him. He's sexy. He's got these beautiful eyes. She's no stranger to having a one night stand. It's just sex. But she promised Livie she wouldn't have sex with strangers any more. But she's having a hard time keeping that promise with the hot as hell Trent showing up every where. Her gym, her work and even when she's doing laundry. After a scare in her apartment and Trent comes to the rescue Kacey thinks things are heating up between her and her sexy neighbor. But Trent has other plans. He sees past these walls Kacey has put up. He wants to take things slow with her even if it is the hardest thing he's had to do. <br />Trent wants Kacey to open up about her past. Kacey is fine keeping that shit buried deep! She definitely doesn't want to talk about it. She thinks everyone is crazy talking about their tragic past. But Trent will try everything to get Kacey to open up and trust him. <br /><br />“Give me your heart, Kacey. I’ll take everything that comes with it.”~Trent<br /><br />“I’ll make you whole again, Kacey. I promise you, I will,” ~Trent<br /><br />I loved Trent. One minute he was slow and sweet and the next he was taking control of the wheel. But Trent's past is also messed up. <br /><br />So I had my suspicions about Trent but I kept thinking no it can't be him. So I kept reading. Then I was loving all the others in the book and wanted to see if we get their stories so I'm on GRs checking for other books. That's when I see the 0.5 book and I'm like damn! O.O!<br /><br />When Trents past catches up with him my heart was breaking for both him and Kacey. The tears were flowing. The scene behind the glass tore me up!!!<br /><br />Then I found myself rooting for both of them to get better. I needed them to get better! <br /><br />The ending had my tears flowing again. They were happy tears though. <br />What can I say? My feelings were a mess during this book. It was well worth losing sleep and walking around like a zombie today! Loved it!!<br /><br />My very first read by this author and I will be reading more in this series. I loved Livie and am so glad her story is next. <br /><br />Seizing him. Feeling him. Loving him.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12394509584834911929" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Ugi6hqUvWutA6Bb98jLDK/IasEG+9NyFJsFAVbshc5ghWH/jIgCevQMH0faGrSbA1aXUjR4daUEfsBtQB43BeQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('eQejUd/HupKEnbZziUSr7KUdrndoYstNWdlMHInhCEEKV2Y0WOh+xMdycXj9204HgqLKu8iLfolgqBcZNU26oA==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText14789168553887609489" style="display:none">K.A. Tucker writes captivating stories with an edge.<br /><br />She is the internationally bestselling author of the Ten Tiny Breaths and Burying Water series, He Will Be My Ruin, Until It Fades, Keep Her Safe, The Simple Wild, Be the Girl, and Say You Still Love Me. Her books have been featured in national publications including USA Today, Globe &amp; Mail, Suspense Magazine, Publisher's Weekly, Oprah Mag, and First for Women. She has been nominated for the Goodreads Choice Award for Best Romance 2013 for TEN TINY BREATHS and Best Romance 2018 for THE SIMPLE WILD. KEEP HER SAFE made Suspense Magazine's Best of 2018 list for Romantic Suspense.<br /><br />K.A.
